Tennis_004	Decrease your opponent's stamina by making\nthem chase your shots back and forth. Whoever\ntires out their opponent first has the advantage.
TennisTitle_005	When Your Stamina Gets Low
Tennis_005	As your stamina decreases, you're more likely to hit wobbly\nshots. Watch for this when a rally lasts a long time.
TennisTitle_006	Smashes
Tennis_006	A wobbly ball is your chance for a {color[0200]}Smash{color[ffff]}. Focus and slam it in!
TennisTitle_007	Adding Topspin
Tennis_007	To hit a ball with topspin, {color[0200]}twist your wrist\nover the ball {color[ffff]}the moment you hit it.
TennisTitle_008	Adding Backspin
Tennis_008	To hit a ball with backspin, {color[0200]}twist your wrist like you're\nscooping from below {color[ffff]}the moment you hit it.
TennisTitle_009	Using Spin Effectively
Tennis_009	Backspin will make the ball curve slightly. Topspin\nincreases ball velocity and makes it bounce quicker.
TennisTitle_010	How to Hit a Lob
Tennis_010	{color[0200]}Swing {color[ffff]}the Joy-Con {color[0200]}from low to high {color[ffff]}to send\nthe ball over your opponent's head for a Lob!
TennisTitle_011	Three Types of Tennis Courts
Tennis_011	The ball will {color[0200]}move {color[ffff]}differently {color[0200]}after bouncing {color[ffff]}depending\non the type of court you're playing on.
TennisTitle_012	Hard Courts
Tennis_012	Hard courts are pink. They're {color[0200]}standard courts {color[ffff]}where the ball will\nbounce high and speed won't drop much after bouncing.
TennisTitle_013	Clay Courts
Tennis_013	Clay courts are brown. The ball will slow down\nafter it bounces and {color[0200]}rallies tend to last longer{color[ffff]},\nso choose your shots strategically.
TennisTitle_014	Grass Courts
Tennis_014	Grass courts are green. They're the {color[0200]}hardest to maintain long\nrallies on {color[ffff]}because the ball bounces low without losing speed.
TennisTitle_015	Hitting the Ball Out
Tennis_015	If you hit a backspin shot when you're at the net,\n{color[0200]}it's easy to send the ball out-of-bounds{color[ffff]}. Be careful!
BowlingTitle_000	Hook
Bowling_000	{color[0200]}Twist the{color[ffff]} Joy-Con {color[0200]}slightly when you swing {color[ffff]}to bowl a Hook!\nThe ball will curve in that direction before it reaches the pins.
BowlingTitle_001	Adjust Your Position
Bowling_001	Use the {color[0200]} Stick {color[ffff]}to move yourself to a\nposition where it's easier to aim for the pins.
BowlingTitle_002	Aim Your Throw
Bowling_002	Use {color[0200]} and {color[ffff]} to adjust the direction of your\nthrow to make it easier to aim for the pins.
BowlingTitle_003	In Case of Split...
Bowling_003	When nonadjacent pins are left standing, it's called a {color[0200]}Split{color[ffff]}.\nAim for the outside edge of a pin so it can knock over the other.
BowlingTitle_004	Zooming the Camera
Bowling_004	You can use {color[0200]} to zoom in{color[ffff]}. This is helpful if you need\nto take a good look at a special lane before bowling.
BowlingTitle_005	Proper Bowling Form
Bowling_005	{color[0200]}After readying the ball at your chest{color[ffff]}, mimic the\nactual motions of bowling as much as possible.\nFundamentals are important!

ProgramMsg\Tips.msbt
TipsTitle_000	Tourist Tip: Spocco Square Amenities
Tips_000	After a full day of playing sports, you'll have easy access to\nshopping, restaurants, and work, no matter which area you're in.
TipsTitle_001	Tourist Tip: Official Gear
Tips_001	There are eight colors of official sportswear that anybody can use.\nJoin the match in your favorite!
TipsTitle_002	Tourist Tip: Official Sporting Goods
Tips_002	One of each type of sporting equipment (rackets, etc.) is available.\nChallenge yourself to a new sport, and try some of them out!
TipsTitle_003	Tourist Tip: Sportsmates
Tips_003	The folks that enjoy all the competition in Spocco Square are\nnicknamed "Sportsmates."
TipsTitle_004	Tourist Tip: Background Music
Tips_004	The background music playing in each area is chosen to match the\nfeel of the sport that is played there.
TipsTitle_005	Tourist Tip: Collaboration Items
Tips_005	Some earnable items are the result of collaborations with\nSpocco Square businesses. They're only available for a limited\ntime, so be sure to check every week.
TipsTitle_006	Tourist Tip: Sports Technology Institute
Tips_006	At the Sports Technology Institute near the tennis courts, they're\ndeveloping advances like perfectly transparent walls that keep\nsoccer balls from flying off the field.
TipsTitle_007	Tourist Tip: Futuristic Sports Tech
Tips_007	When you play Tennis by yourself, Spocco Square's state-of-\nthe-art courts can provide a holographic doubles partner!
TipsTitle_008	Tourist Tip: Shuttle Buses
Tips_008	There's a red bus going between the venues every 15 minutes.
TipsTitle_009	Tourist Tip: Banners
Tips_009	Each area has banners displayed for the relevant sport.\nLook for them before a match starts or during a replay.
TipsTitle_010	Tourist Tip: Limited-Time Items
Tips_010	After playing a sport, you'll receive points toward limited-availability\nitems! Collect them to customize your character.
TipsTitle_011	Tourist Tip: Volleyball Area
Tips_011	There's an art gallery directly underneath the court. You may\nfind it useful as a conversation starter with your teammate.
TipsTitle_012	Tourist Tip: Soccer Area
Tips_012	This area has a large field and a small field. You might be able to\nsee one from the edge of the other.
TipsTitle_013	Tourist Tip: Badminton Area
Tips_013	The owner of Cafe Buttons loves cats! But if you see their cats,\nplease don't feed them (they're on a special diet).
TipsTitle_014	Tourist Tip: Volleyball Area
Tips_014	When visitors are looking for a place to enjoy a delicious hot drink\nand a book, they look no further than humhum books!
TipsTitle_015	Tourist Tip: Badminton Area
Tips_015	The cafe building here was made from a freight container! Highly\nrecommended for the fan of small, enclosed spaces.
TipsTitle_016	Tourist Tip: Badminton Area
Tips_016	Ice Cream Volley's second location is in this area.\nDo you know where the first one is?
TipsTitle_017	Tourist Tip: Tennis Area
Tips_017	After competitors have worked up a sweat playing Tennis, they often\nhead to the Lotus Juice Bar just off the courts! They've got a great\nselection of smoothies and healthy soups.
TipsTitle_018	Tourist Tip: Soccer Area
Tips_018	The inspiration for the soccer area was "where culture and sports\nmeet." The library overlooking the field has a huge sports-history\nsection.
TipsTitle_019	Tourist Tip: Soccer Area
Tips_019	The display next to the elevator shows things such as PR videos for\nvarious Spocco Square stores.
TipsTitle_020	Tourist Tip: Chambara Area
Tips_020	Hotel Spocco has a total of 25 luxurious rooms. Their soft beds are\nperfect for collapsing into after a full day of playing sports!
TipsTitle_021	Tourist Tip: Chambara Area
Tips_021	The red brick warehouse where the Chambara platform is located\nwas built 100 years ago when this area was a port.
TipsTitle_022	Tourist Tip: Chambara Area
Tips_022	When the central Chambara platform has been removed for\nmaintenance, there are sometimes artistic-swimming events\nin the pool below.
TipsTitle_023	Tourist Tip: Tennis Area
Tips_023	The greens around the Tennis area are a popular spot for a stroll.\nIf you lie down on the lawn, you can actually hear the sound of balls\nbouncing on the court.
TipsTitle_024	Tourist Tip: Tennis Area
Tips_024	There are drones operating 24 hours a day to collect the tennis\nballs that end up in the pool surrounding the tennis court.
TipsTitle_025	Tourist Tip: Bowling Area
Tips_025	The Bowling area is located inside the shopping mall. Visitors often\nstop for a game while they're shopping for souvenirs!
TipsTitle_026	Tourist Tip: Bowling Area
Tips_026	The bowling alley sports a large skylight so you can soak up the\nsunlight while you play!
TipsTitle_027	Tourist Tip: Volleyball Area
Tips_027	The building here was remodeled from a large warehouse.\nWarm sunlight streams in through the glass ceiling.
TipsTitle_028	Tourist Tip: Bowling Area
Tips_028	The sofas in the bowling alley are a comfortable place to relax and\nwatch the action. Visitors can even have food and drinks brought to\nthem there.
TipsTitle_029	Tourist Tip: Bowling Area
Tips_029	Mount & Co., next to the bowling alley, is an outfitter that\nspecializes in camping gear and boats.
TipsTitle_030	Tourist Tip: Central Plaza
Tips_030	The central plaza with the large "S" landmark has a reception area\nfor visitors and locker rooms for competitors.
